   var deviceType = {
        desktop: (window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth) > 767 ? true : false,
        mobile: (window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth) > 767 ? false : true
      };

      window.googletag = window.googletag || {cmd: []};

      // Desktop/Table google display ads
      if (deviceType.desktop) {

        googletag.cmd.push(function() {
          googletag.defineSlot('/1058709/SDReader_Default_ROS_500x500_Popup', [500, 500], 'div-gpt-ad-1581969377769-0').addService(googletag.pubads());

          // Detect if slot was filled with an AD
          googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() === 'div-gpt-ad-1581969377769-0' && !event.isEmpty) {
              displayPopupWithAd();
            }
          });

          googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
          googletag.enableServices();
        });

        googletag.cmd.push(function() {
          googletag.defineSlot('/1058709/SDR_PageFooter_728x90', [728, 90], 'div-gpt-ad-1589326896462-0').addService(googletag.pubads());
          googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
          googletag.enableServices();
        });

          // Detect if slot was filled with an AD

          googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
          googletag.enableServices();
        });
      }

      function displayPopupWithAd() {
        if (Cookies.get('readerhouse')) {
          // has already been shown in the last 24 hours
        } else {
          // Display popup ad
          document.getElementById('Popup_Ad').style.display = 'block';
          Cookies.set('readerhouse', 'true', {expires: 1}); // expires: days
        }
      }

   $(document).ready(function(){
        var targetClassName = 'read-time-calculate';

        $('.' + targetClassName).each(function (index) {
          var $this = $(this);
          var totalWords = $this.data('wordcount');
          var timeToRead = Math.round(totalWords / 200); // 200 words per minute is average read time

          // update span child inside target
          $this.children('span').text(timeToRead);
        });
      });
  </script>
